### Kingdom of Dale ###
k_dale = {
	6977.1.1 = { 
		holder = lineofdale46 # Bard the Bowman, King of Dale
	}
	7010.1.1 = { 
		holder = lineofdale48 # Bain
		effect = { # Set court tongue to Westron
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = holder
					has_dlc_feature = royal_court
				}
				holder = {
					set_court_language = language_westron
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { knows_court_language_of = this } }
						learn_court_language_of = this
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	7040.1.1 = { 
		holder = lineofdale50 # Brand
	}
}
